# Event Routing


# HOLDING


# MISC

.EDCT .MSG $aircraft *** ADVISORY *** This route is under a Traffic Management Delay Program from VATUSA. Your assigned departure (takeoff) time is $1. Time now $time. Monitor DEL freq for possible amendments prior to calling GND for taxi. Contact GND 5-7min prior to your departure time, ready for taxi. Advise ATC if unable to meet assigned time or with questions. *** END ***

.MAD .MSG $aircraft *** We understand your frustration with this time restriction. However, the field you are flying to can only support so many arrivals and departures within a certain time and maintain appropriate separation from other aircraft. To help mitigate traffic congestion, VATUSA is establishing more realistic delay programs like this. More specific questions should be directed to VATUSA86 via private message in your pilot client.

#EQUIPMENT SUFFIX CODES
.EQUIPH .MSG FAA_ISR *** /H __ Failed transponder or Failed Mode C capability
.EQUIPW .MSG FAA_ISR *** /W __ XPDR-Y __ MODE C-Y __ RNAV-N __ GNSS-N __ RVSM-Y
.EQUIPZ .MSG FAA_ISR *** /Z __ XPDR-Y __ MODE C-Y __ RNAV-Y __ GNSS-N __ RVSM-Y
.EQUIPL .MSG FAA_ISR *** /L __ XPDR-Y __ MODE C-Y __ RNAV-Y __ GNSS-Y __ RVSM-Y								 
.EQUIPX .MSG FAA_ISR *** /X __ XPDR-N __ MODE C-N __ RNAV-N __ GNSS-N __ RVSM-N __ DME-N
.EQUIPT .MSG FAA_ISR *** /T __ XPDR-Y __ MODE C-N __ RNAV-N __ GNSS-N __ RVSM-N __ DME-N
.EQUIPU .MSG FAA_ISR *** /U __ XPDR-Y __ MODE C-Y __ RNAV-N __ GNSS-N __ RVSM-N __ DME-N

# "Trouble Pilot"
.PRC .MSG ZLC_ISR With all due respect, it appears that there is a significant amount of knowledge that is still required on your part to complete flights like this on the network per the VATSIM Expectations and Requirements for Pilots. Please navigate to the VATSIM Pilot Resource Center site and start there.
.TIPS .msg ZLC_ISR There has been 1 or more encounters with you that would make us think you might benefit from some resources we have posted on our site to help pilots with misc procedures. It is our Tips for Pilots section. Take a look at it sometime. Have a great day! zlcartcc.com
.WHATRWY .MSG ZLC_ISR After you get your clearance, it is standard for pilots to program their main route and leave off the SID portion in the FMS because they usually do not get their RWY assignment until they notify the ATC of their position on the field and request taxi. Then during taxi, the pilot then programs the rest of the SID portion. So you will get that information when you call for taxi.
.TWRFREQ .MSG ZLC_ISR Upon reaching the departure runway and ready to request takeoff, you are expected to change to the appropriate frequency for Tower on your own, without being told to do so. Reference the Federal Aviation Administration Aeronautical Information Manual 4-3-14.a https://www.faa.gov/air_traffic/publications/atpubs/aim_html/chap4_section_3.html#$paragraph4-3-14

# Military
.OVERHEAD .MSG ZLC_ISR Overhead_Manuever_Phraseology*** WIND ### @ ##. PATTERN ALTITUDE ###. (Right/Left) TURNS. REPORT INITIAL RUNWAY ##. ____ [Initial Report] BREAK AT (numbers/midfield/departure end). REPORT BREAK. ____ [Break Report] CHECK GEAR DOWN. RWY ## CLEARED TO LAND.
.MILCT .MSG ZLC_ISR Military Takeoff Clearance*** Military aircraft (except Cargo and Transport types), WIND---@-- RWY-- CLEARED FOR TAKEOFF
.MILCL .MSG ZLC_ISR Wind $wind($arr). Check Wheels Down. RWY ## Cleared to Land.

# Released for Departure (Uncontrolled Field)
.RFD .MSG ZLC_ISR *** $aircraft Released for departure. Clearance void if not off by $ftime(10). If not off by $ftime(10), advise $radioname() on $freq() not later than $ftime(15) of intentions. Time now- $time. Frequency change approved.

# Holding instructions
.HOLDING .MSG ZLC_ISR *** HOLD (direction) OF (waypoint). ON THE (radial, course, bearing, track, azimuth, airway, or route).(leg length of hold if applicable).(state Left Turns, if right turns are not to be assumed).MAINTAIN (altitude).EXPECT FURTHER CLEARANCE (time).

# IFR Procedures Phraseology Help
.OTP .MSG ZLC_ISR *** CLIMB TO AND REPORT REACHING VFR ON TOP, TOPS REPORTED (altitude, if none "NO TOPS REPORTED"), IF NOT ON TOP AT (altitude), MAINTAIN (altitude), AND ADVISE. MAINTAIN VFR ON TOP.

# Notifications
.DNM .MSG $atccallsign($1) *** $dep _ $aircraft _ $type($aircraft) _ $2 $3 _ $4 $5 $6 _ $route _ $alt
.ANM .MSG $atccallsign($1) *** $arr _ $aircraft _ $2 $3 $4 $5 $6
.RC .MSG $atccallsign($1) *** $aircraft Rolling _ $2 $3 $4 $5 $6
.RT .MSG $atccallsign($1) *** $aircraft Rejected Takeoff _ $2 $3 $4 $5 $6

# Departure Release Requests
.RR .MSG $atccallsign($1) *** REQUEST RELEASE- $aircraft _ $dep to $arr _ $2 $3 $4 $5 $6 _ $route
.RA .MSG $atccallsign($1) *** $aircraft RELEASED @ $ftime($2)

# Other
.M .MSG $atccallsign($1) *** $aircraft _ $2 $3 $4 $5 $6
.MA .MSG $atccallsign($1) *** $aircraft ***Missed Approach***. $2
.po .msg $atccallsign($1) *** POINTOUT *** for $aircraft $dist($2) $bear($2) of $uc($2) ::: $3 $4 $5 $6 $7 $8 $9
.ho .msg $atccallsign($1) *** HANDOFF *** $dist($2) $bear($2) of $uc($2), $squawk is $aircraft at $calt ::: $3 $4 $5 $6 $7 $8 $9
.apreq .msg $atccallsign($1) *** APREQ *** $aircraft ::: $2 $3 $4 $5 $6 $7 $8 $9
.DT .MSG $atccallsign($1) *** $aircraft _ Landed $time
.MSOMC Missoula airspace is my control.
.MSORLS Missoula airspace released as requested.

# General Commands
.WHERE .AN DBL
.NOAN .noanchors
.DOF .rsb $dep $arr
.METAR .msg ZLC_ISR *** $metar($1)
.W .MSG ZLC_ISR K$1 Wind $wind(K$1) ::: Altimeter $altim(K$1)
.WW .MSG ZLC_ISR ::: $dep Wind $wind($dep) _ A$altim($dep) --------------- $arr Wind $wind($arr) _ A$altim($arr)
.OBSVIS .VIS KSLC KBOI KBZN MLS
.CTRVIS .VIS KBOI KBZN KSLC MLS

.ZLCAT .AUTOTRACK KBIL KBOI KBZN KGPI KGTF KOGD KPVU KSLC KMSO

.S56AT .AUTOTRACK KSLC KOGD KPVU
.STOPS56AT .AUTOTRACK -KSLC -KOGD -KPVU
.RLSFP .msg fp $aircraft release

#                        TEXT TO PILOTS
#######################################################################
#######################################################################
#######################################################################


# General
.tnew .msg $aircraft Hello, it appears you may be new to the network. First of all - welcome to VATSIM! It may be tempting to jump right ahead and fly, but I would suggest you read through some documents first, in order to prepare yourself for what you may encounter. First of all - you should read the VATSIM tutorials at vats.im/prc. Here you can find everything you need. Second of all, you should read through the VATSIM Code of Conduct (vats.im/coc), especially sections A and B, in order to not get in trouble for something you didn't know. Let me know if you have any other questions, thanks for flying today!
.tsq Squawk $squawk
.tcon Contact $radioname($1) on $freq($1).
.tmon Monitor $radioname($1) on $freq($1).
.tCLOSING  ****NOTAM $radioname() is closing in $1 minutes. ****
.tCLOSED  ****NOTAM $radioname() closed at $time Zulu. ****
.tprc With all due respect, it appears that there is a significant amount of knowledge that is still required on your part to complete flights like this on the network per the VATSIM Expectations and Requirements for Pilots. Please navigate to the VATSIM Pilot Resource Center site and start there.
.THOTMIC ATTENTION ALL AIRCRAFT: Someone is continuing to press the MIC button. Please check your connections and resolve this issue as it is disrupting communications on this frequency.
.TTIPS There has been 1 or more encounters with you that would make us think you might benefit from some resources we have posted on our site to help pilots with misc procedures. It is our Tips for Pilots section. Take a look at it sometime. Have a great day! zlcartcc.com
.TWHATRWY After you get your clearance, it is standard for pilots to program their main route and leave off the SID portion in the FMS because they usually do not get their RWY assignment until they notify the ATC of their position on the field and request taxi. Then during taxi, the pilot then programs the rest of the SID portion. So you will get that information when you call for taxi.
.TTWRFREQ .msg $aircraft Upon reaching the departure runway and ready to request takeoff, you are expected to change to the appropriate frequency for Tower on your own, without being told to do so. Reference the Federal Aviation Administration Aeronautical Information Manual 4-3-14.a https://www.faa.gov/air_traffic/publications/atpubs/aim_html/chap4_section_3.html#$paragraph4-3-14
.TEQUIP .msg $aircraft What is your equipment suffix code? ***I am NOT asking for your Aircraft Code: "$type($aircraft)"*** If you need help, visit this website: https://equipment-suffix.febuddy.com/
.TPDC? The message you got via private message is a way of simulating a real world system called Controller Pilot Data Link Communications (CPDLC). At certain airports in the real world, your departure clearance is provided via this system without the need for any voice communications. If you don't have any questions concerning the clearance, just prepare your aircraft with that information and report to Ground Control when ready for taxi, squawking your assigned code.
.TNnumber .msg $aircraft Your callsign seems to be not valid. This link assists you format your callsign per USA regulation. Thank you for the help! https://www.faa.gov/licenses_certificates/aircraft_certification/aircraft_registry/forming_nnumber/

# Clearance Delivery
.trbc Read Back Correct.

# General CRAFT
.TCRAFTU Cleared to $arr via $route. Departure frequency is with UNICOM 122.800, squawk $squawk
.TCRAFT Cleared to $arr. Fly heading $1 expect radar vectors on course $route. Maint $2. Departure frequency $freq($3), squawk $squawk
.TNOPDC .msg $aircraft ***ADVISORY*** A Pre-Departure Clearance (PDC) was unable to be sent to you due to a lack of sufficient information in your flight plan. Please contact $radioname($1) on $freq($1) for your clearance delivery.

# Ground
.trtv Runway $uc($1), taxi via $2 $3
.ttpv Taxi to parking via $1 $2

# Tower
.tcl Runway $uc($1), Wind $winds, cleared to land.
.tct Runway $uc($1), Wind $winds, cleared for takeoff.

# Radar-General
.tsqi squawk $squawk and ident
.trc Radar Contact
.tfh Fly heading $1
.ttl Turn left heading $1
.ttr Turn right heading $1
.trst Radar Services Terminated
.tcm Climb and maintain $1
.tdm Descend and maintain $1

# Departure
.thfr Hold for release.
.trfd Released for departure. Clearance void if not off by $ftime(10). If not off by $ftime(10), advise $radioname() on $freq() not later than $ftime(15) of intentions. Time now- $time Zulu. Frequency change approved.

# Approach
.tptac $dist($1) miles from $uc($1), Fly heading $2. Maintain $3 until established on the localizer. Cleared $4 runway $5 approach.
.tptacils $dist($1) miles from $uc($1), Fly heading $2. Maintain $3 until established on the localizer. Cleared ILS runway $4 approach.
.trfis Airport is at your $oclock($arr), $dist($arr) miles, report in sight
.tcva Cleared visual runway $1 approach.

# En-Route
.trcdb Radar Contact $dist($1) miles $bear($1) of $uc($1)
.tlma Leaving my airspace, radar service terminated, frequency change approved.
